/// Logic
class Main
{
Description = "Collect all the candies on the map in the shortest amount of time.";
StartDelay = 5.0;
EndAfterWin = true;
InfiniteLives = true;
Lives = 0;
RespawnDelay = 1.5;
_CollectiblesCurrent = 0;
_CollectiblesTotal = 0;
_started = false;
_startBarriers = null;
_dieTimeLeft = 0.0;
_livesLeft = 0;
_finished = false;
_hasSpawned = false;
_SpawnPosition = Vector3(0,0,0);

function OnGameStart()
{
self._startBarriers = Map.FindMapObjectsByTag("RacingStartBarrier");
self._livesLeft = self.Lives;
Network.MyPlayer.SetCustomProperty("NoLivesLeft", false);
Game.SetPlaylist("Racing");
}
function OnCharacterSpawn(character)
{
self._SpawnPosition = character.Position;
}
function FinishRace(human)
{
if (!self._finished)
{
Game.PrintAll(human.Player.Name + " collected all the candies in " + String.FormatFloat(Time.GameTime - self.StartDelay, 2));
Network.SendMessage(Network.MasterClient, "Finish");
self._finished = true;
}
}

function OnNetworkMessage(sender, message)
{
if (Network.IsMasterClient && message == "Finish" && !Game.IsEnding && self.EndAfterWin)
{
UI.SetLabelAll(UILabelEnum.MiddleCenter, sender.Name + " has collected all the candy in " + String.FormatFloat(Time.GameTime - self.StartDelay, 2) + "seconds!");
Game.End(10);
}
}

function OnCharacterDie(victim, killer, killerName)
{
if (victim.IsMainCharacter)
{
self._dieTimeLeft = self.RespawnDelay;
}
}


function OnTick()
{
if (!self._started)
{
Game.SpawnPlayer(Network.MyPlayer, false);
UI.SetLabel(UILabelEnum.TopCenter, "Collect " + Convert.ToString(self._CollectiblesTotal) + " Candies In: " + String.FormatFloat(self.StartDelay - Time.GameTime, 2));
if (Time.GameTime > self.StartDelay)
{
self._started = true;
for (barrier in self._startBarriers)
{
barrier.Active = false;
}
if (Network.MyPlayer.Status == PlayerStatusEnum.Alive)
{
self._hasSpawned = true;
}
}
if (Network.MyPlayer.Character != null)
{
Network.MyPlayer.Character.Position = self._SpawnPosition;
Network.MyPlayer.Character.Velocity = Vector3(0,0,0);
Network.MyPlayer.Character.RightHookEnabled = false;
Network.MyPlayer.Character.LeftHookEnabled = false;
}
}
else
{
if (Network.MyPlayer.Character != null)
{
Network.MyPlayer.Character.RightHookEnabled = true;
Network.MyPlayer.Character.LeftHookEnabled = true;
}
if (!self.InfiniteLives)
{
UI.SetLabel(UILabelEnum.TopCenter, "Time: " + String.FormatFloat(Time.GameTime - self.StartDelay, 2) + ", Lives: " + Convert.ToString(self._livesLeft) + String.Newline +
"Candies: " + Convert.ToString(self._CollectiblesCurrent) + " / " + Convert.ToString(self._CollectiblesTotal));
}
else
{
UI.SetLabel(UILabelEnum.TopCenter, "Time: " + String.FormatFloat(Time.GameTime - self.StartDelay, 2) + String.Newline +
"Candies: " + Convert.ToString(self._CollectiblesCurrent) + " / " + Convert.ToString(self._CollectiblesTotal));
}
self._dieTimeLeft = self._dieTimeLeft - Time.TickTime;
if (!self._hasSpawned && Network.MyPlayer.Status == PlayerStatusEnum.Dead)
{
Game.SpawnPlayer(Network.MyPlayer, false);
self._hasSpawned = true;
}
elif (Network.MyPlayer.Status == PlayerStatusEnum.Dead && self._dieTimeLeft <= 0.0)
{
if (self._livesLeft > 0 || self.InfiniteLives)
{
Game.SpawnPlayer(Network.MyPlayer, false);
self._livesLeft = self._livesLeft - 1;
}
else
{
Network.MyPlayer.SetCustomProperty("NoLivesLeft", true);
}
}
if (Network.IsMasterClient && !Game.IsEnding)
{
anyPlayerAlive = false;
anyPlayerSpawned = false;
for (player in Network.Players)
{
if (player.Status != PlayerStatusEnum.Spectating)
{
anyPlayerSpawned = true;
noLivesLeft = player.GetCustomProperty("NoLivesLeft");
if (player.Status == PlayerStatusEnum.Alive || (noLivesLeft != null && !noLivesLeft))
{
anyPlayerAlive = true;
}
}
}
if (anyPlayerSpawned && !anyPlayerAlive)
{
UI.SetLabelAll(UILabelEnum.MiddleCenter, "All players have no lives left.");
Game.End(10);
}
}
}
}
}
component Collectible
{
_Collected = false;

function Init()
{
Main._CollectiblesTotal += 1;
}
function OnCollisionEnter(other)
{
if (other.IsMainCharacter && self._Collected == false)
{
self._Collected = true;
Main._CollectiblesCurrent += 1;
self.MapObject.Scale = Vector3(0,0,0);
other.CurrentGas = other.CurrentGas + 5.0;
Game.SpawnEffect(EffectNameEnum.CriticalHit, self.MapObject.Position, self.MapObject.Rotation, 3.0);
other.PlaySound(HumanSoundEnum.Checkpoint);
}
if (Main._CollectiblesCurrent == Main._CollectiblesTotal)
{
Main.FinishRace(other);
}
}
}
